OBJECT Report 11012806 Cost Plus Sheet Service Order
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=;
    Time=;
    Version List=4PS14.00;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=[DEU=Regieeintrag-Blatt Serviceauftrag;
               ENU=Cost Plus Sheet Service Order;
               NLD=Verrekenstaat serviceorder];
    OnInitReport=BEGIN
                   GLSetup.GET;
                   GLSetup.TESTFIELD("LCY Code");
                   GLSetup.TESTFIELD("Amount Rounding Precision");

                   CompanyInfo.GET;
                   FormatAddr.Company(CompanyAddr,CompanyInfo);
                 END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 1100525000;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012823;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(No.);
               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  ServOrdFilter@1100528400 : Code[20];
                                BEGIN

                                  //Set Service Order Filter. Not used for FlowFields but for the link to the other dataitems
                                  IF CollectBaseSo THEN BEGIN
                                    IF NOT "Base Service Order" AND (GETFILTER("Base Service Order No.") = '') THEN
                                      MESSAGE(Text007, "No.");
                                    FillServiceOrderFilter(ServOrdFilter, "Base Service Order")
                                  END ELSE
                                    FillServiceOrderFilter(ServOrdFilter, FALSE);
                                  SETFILTER("Service Order Filter", ServOrdFilter);

                                  IF NOT ServOrderExtension.GET("No.") THEN
                                    ServOrderExtension.INIT;  //DP00106

                                  TempVATAmountLine.DELETEALL;

                                  CLEAR(AmountSSInc);
                                  CLEAR("AmountSS incl.VAT");

                                  IF "Customer No." <> CustomerRec."No." THEN BEGIN
                                    CustomerRec.GET("Customer No.");
                                    IF CustomerRec."Currency Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                      CurrRec.GET(CustomerRec."Currency Code");
                                      CurrRec.TESTFIELD("Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
                                      CurrRec.TESTFIELD("Amount Rounding Precision");
                                      IF CustomerRec."Currency Code" <> GLSetup."LCY Code" THEN
                                        "Currency Factor" := CurrencyExchRate.ExchangeRate(
                                          0, '', WORKDATE,CustomerRec."Currency Code",TRUE)
                                      ELSE
                                        "Currency Factor" := 0;
                                      TotalText := STRSUBSTNO(Text001,CustomerRec."Currency Code");
                                      TotalInclVATText := STRSUBSTNO(Text002,CustomerRec."Currency Code");
                                      AmountRoundPrecision := CurrRec."Amount Rounding Precision";
                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                      "Currency Factor" := 0;
                                      TotalText := STRSUBSTNO(Text001,GLSetup."LCY Code");
                                      TotalInclVATText := STRSUBSTNO(Text002,GLSetup."LCY Code");
                                      AmountRoundPrecision := GLSetup."Amount Rounding Precision";
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  CLEAR(CustomerAddress);
                                  IF CustomerRec.GET("Customer No.") THEN BEGIN
                                    FormatAddr.Customer(CustomerAddress,CustomerRec);
                                    CustomerPhoneNo := CustomerRec."Phone No.";
                                    CustomerFaxNo := CustomerRec."Fax No.";
                                  END;

                                  CurrReport.PAGENO := 1;
                                  CLEAR(PrintSubTotal);

                                  ServiceText.SETRANGE("Table Name",ServiceText."Table Name"::"Service Order");
                                  ServiceText.SETRANGE("No.", "No.");
                                  ServiceText.SETRANGE("Table Field",90);
                                  ServiceText.SETFILTER("Line No.",'<>%1',0);
                                  IF ServiceText.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                                    REPEAT
                                      ServOrderExtensionProblemText += ServiceText.Comment;
                                    UNTIL ServiceText.NEXT = 0;
                                  END;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=No. }

               DataItemTable=Table11012825;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Service Order No.,Line No.)
                                 WHERE(Cost Type=CONST(Labor));
               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF NOT ProcessCostPlusEntries(
                                           Quantity,"Basic Price (LCY)","Sales Price (LCY)","Invoice Price (LCY)",
                                           "VAT Prod. Posting Group",Invoiced,Chargeable)
                                  THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;  //db, 28-06-10: M15293

                                  ShowLaborLine := FALSE;
                                  ShowLaborTotal := FALSE;

                                  IF (PrintProcessedLines) OR (NOT Invoiced AND NOT PrintProcessedLines) THEN
                                    ShowLaborLine := TRUE;

                                  IF (PrintProcessedLines) OR (NOT Invoiced AND NOT PrintProcessedLines) THEN
                                    ShowLaborTotal := TRUE;
                                END;

               OnPostDataItem=BEGIN
                                EmptyTotalsByCostType;
                              END;

               DataItemLinkReference=Service Order;
               DataItemLink=Service Order No.=FIELD(Service Order Filter),
                            Base Service Order No.=FIELD(Base Service Order No.) }

    { 1100525009;1;DataItem;Total            ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 WHERE(Number=CONST(1));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF NOT PrintTotal THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                               PrintTotal := FALSE;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  // Melding 23438.Start
                                  IF TempVATAmountLine.COUNT = 1 THEN BEGIN
                                    TempVATAmountLine.FIND('-');
                                    TotalVATText := STRSUBSTNO(Text006,TempVATAmountLine."VAT %")
                                  END ELSE
                                    TotalVATText := Text005;
                                  // Melding 23438.End
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525068;2;Column;TotalText_Total    ;
               SourceExpr=TotalText }

    { 1100409056;2;Column;VATAmountText_Total;
               SourceExpr=TempVATAmountLine.VATAmountText }

    { 1100525070;2;Column;TotalInclVATText_Total;
               SourceExpr=TotalInclVATText }

    { 1100409057;2;Column;AmountExclVat_Total;
               SourceExpr=AmountSSInc }

    { 1100409058;2;Column;VATAmount_Total    ;
               SourceExpr="AmountSS incl.VAT" - AmountSSInc }

    { 1100409059;2;Column;AmountInclVat_Total;
               SourceExpr="AmountSS incl.VAT" }

    { 1100525010;1;DataItem;VATCounter       ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF TempVATAmountLine.COUNT <= 1 THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                               SETRANGE(Number,1,TempVATAmountLine.COUNT);
                               CurrReport.CREATETOTALS(TempVATAmountLine."VAT Base",TempVATAmountLine."VAT Amount");
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  TempVATAmountLine.GetLine(Number);
                                END;

    PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    PROCEDURE ProcessCostPlusEntries@16(Quantity@11012000 : Decimal;VAR "Basic Price"@11012001 : Decimal;VAR "Sales Price"@11012002 : Decimal;"Invoice Price"@1100485000 : Decimal;"VAT Prod. Posting Group"@11012003 : Code[10];Invoiced@1210190000 : Boolean;Chargeable@1100525000 : Boolean) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      IF Invoiced AND NOT PrintProcessedLines THEN EXIT(FALSE);  //db, 28-06-10: M15293

      IF NOT Invoiced AND NOT Chargeable AND PrintChargeableLinesOnly THEN EXIT (FALSE);  //db, 28-06-10: M15293

      //Convert Unit Price into Customer Currency
      IF CustomerRec."Currency Code" <> GLSetup."LCY Code" THEN
        "Basic Price" :=
          ROUND
            (CurrencyExchRate.ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(
              0, '', WORKDATE,CustomerRec."Currency Code",
              "Basic Price","Currency Factor",TRUE),
              CurrRec."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");

      //Convert Sales Price to Custumer Currency
      IF CustomerRec."Currency Code" <> GLSetup."LCY Code" THEN
        "Sales Price" :=
          ROUND
            (CurrencyExchRate.ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(
              0, '', WORKDATE,CustomerRec."Currency Code",
              "Sales Price","Currency Factor",TRUE),
              CurrRec."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");

      //Calculate Amounts per Settlement Sheet
      AmountInc := "Invoice Price";
      AmountCTInc := AmountCTInc + AmountInc;
      AmountSSInc := AmountSSInc + AmountInc;

      //VAT
      IF NOT VATPostingSetup.GET(CustomerRec."VAT Bus. Posting Group","VAT Prod. Posting Group") THEN
        VATPostingSetup.INIT;
      "VAT %" := VATPostingSetup."VAT %";
      CASE VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type" OF
        VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT",
        VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
          "VAT %" := 0;
      END;

      CASE VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type" OF
        VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT",
        VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT":
          BEGIN
            "VAT Base" := AmountInc;
            "Amount Including VAT" := ROUND(AmountInc + "VAT Base" * "VAT %" / 100,0.00001);
          END;
        VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type"::"Full VAT":
          BEGIN
            "VAT Base" := 0;
            "Amount Including VAT" := AmountInc;
          END;
        VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
      //  Voorlopig niet ondersteund. Is alleen van toepassing op de Amerikaanse markt
          BEGIN
            "VAT Base" := AmountInc;
            "Amount Including VAT" := AmountInc;
          END;
      END;

      "AmountSS incl.VAT" := "AmountSS incl.VAT" + "Amount Including VAT";

      TempVATAmountLine.INIT;
      TempVATAmountLine."VAT Identifier" := VATPostingSetup."VAT Identifier"; // Melding 23438
      TempVATAmountLine."VAT Calculation Type" := VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type"; // Melding 23438
      TempVATAmountLine."VAT %" := "VAT %";
      TempVATAmountLine."VAT Base" := "VAT Base";
      TempVATAmountLine."Amount Including VAT" := "Amount Including VAT";
      TempVATAmountLine.InsertLine;

      PrintTotal := TRUE;

      EXIT(TRUE);  //db, 28-06-10: M15293
    END;

    PROCEDURE EmptyTotalsByCostType@1();
    BEGIN
      AmountCTInc := 0;
    END;

    PROCEDURE FillServiceOrderFilter@1100525000(VAR ServOrdFilter@1100525000 : Code[20];TotalBase@1100525001 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      IF TotalBase THEN
        ServOrdFilter := ''
      ELSE
        ServOrdFilter := "Service Order"."No.";
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value = 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &gt; 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &gt;= 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &lt; 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &lt;= 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Shared offset As Integer
Shared newgroup As Object
Shared currentgroup1 As Object
Shared currentgroup2 As Object
Shared currentgroup3 As Object
Shared currentgroup4 As Object

Public Function GetGroupPageNumber(newgroup2 As Boolean, pagenumber As Integer) As Object
    If newgroup2
        offset = pagenumber - 1
    End If
    Return pagenumber - offset
End Function

Public Function InNewGroup(group1 As Object, group2 As Object, group3 As Object, group4 As Object) As Boolean
    newgroup = False
    If Not (group1 = currentgroup1)
        newgroup = True
        currentgroup4 = group4
        currentgroup3 = group3
        currentgroup2 = group2
        currentgroup1 = group1
    Else
        If Not (group2 = currentgroup2)
            newgroup = True
            currentgroup4 = group4
            currentgroup3 = group3
            currentgroup2 = group2
        Else
            If Not (group3 = currentgroup3)
                newgroup = True
                currentgroup4 = group4
                currentgroup3 = group3
            Else
                If Not (group4 = currentgroup4)
                    newgroup = True
                    currentgroup4 = group4
                End If
            End If
        End If
    End If
    Return newgroup
End Function

Shared Data1 As Object

Public Function GetData(Num As Integer) As Object
    Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data1), Chr(177))))
End Function

Public Function SetData(NewData As Object)
    If NewData &lt;&gt; "" Then
        Data1 = NewData
    End If
End Function
</Code>
  <Language>=User!Language</Language>
  <ConsumeContainerWhitespace>true</ConsumeContainerWhitespace>
  <rd:ReportUnitType>Cm</rd:ReportUnitType>
</Report>
    END_OF_RDLDATA
